                                <div class="zsg-lg-2-3 zsg-md-1-1 hdp-header-description">
                                    <div class="hide zsg-content-component zsg-annotation-area prop-mod prop-notes" id="home-description-fav-note">
                                        <h4>My Notes</h4><span data-zpid="2107410377" class="prop-mod-bd" id="fav-note-text"></span><span class="prop-notes-edit edit-note"><a href="#add-note-code" class="show-lightbox" id="edit-note-btn"> Edit</a></span>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="zsg-content-component">
                                        <div class="notranslate">Looking for a place to build your home and be close to most everything? One of the lots available in the Huron Creek subdivision may be just the place you have been searching for. Several lots with various sizes are available. Convenient location to stores, restaurants and more. Acreage is estimated. Buyer to verify the location of all utility hook-ups as part of an inspection contingency. Notice: Pinehurst, Cedar and Oak Ridge Streets are not developed. Contact City of Houghton for more information regarding future road development if something is built on a parcel. As part of the plat the roads would be considered public but are seasonal and not developed or maintained by any municipality at this time.</div>
